## [May 16, 2025](/content/2025/05/16/README.md)

### Builders / [Google Developer Experts](https://developers.google.com/experts/all/technology/web-technologies)

*   [ngx-schematic-builder (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/kstepien3/ngx-schematic-builder) - A tool for building Angular schematic projects. Compiles and packages your custom schematics, preparing them for publishing and use.

### Free / [Google Developer Experts](https://developers.google.com/experts/all/technology/web-technologies)

*   [ngx-lib-starter-kit (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/r3zafa/ngx-lib-starter-kit) - This boilerplate helps you quickly set up and develop Angular libraries. It includes a pre-configured structure for components, services, utilities, themes, assets, and more. The project is optimized for scalability and maintainability.

Streamline your multilingual development workflow.

### Module Federation / [Google Developer Experts](https://developers.google.com/experts/all/technology/web-technologies)

*   [@module-federation/core (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/module-federation/core) - Module Federation is a concept that allows developers to share code and resources across multiple JavaScript applications.
*   [webpack-module-federation-with-angular (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/edumserrano/webpack-module-federation-with-angular) - Guide to learn about Webpack Module Federation with several Angular code demos.
*   [vite-module-federation-angular-test (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/Seifenn/vite-module-federation-angular-test) - This repository tests the [@module-federation/vite (‚≠ê450)](https://github.com/module-federation/vite) with Angular and AnalogJS, based on the work done in [brandonroberts/angular-vite (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/brandonroberts/angular-vite). It also tests a host with AnalogJS to test SSR. But now the module federation plugin is not compatible with SSR.
*   [angular-microfrontend-demo (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/gioboa/angular-microfrontend-demo) - Module Federation Vite + Angular is now possible.
*   [mfe-crossframework (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/igorhms/mfe-crossframework) - Module Federation project with Angular Host, Cross-framework remotes and without Nx.
*   [backbase-micro-frontends (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/Backbase/backbase-micro-frontends) - Proof of concept showcasing how legacy apps (widgets) can work together with newer apps (journeys) via Module Federation.

### NGXS / [Google Developer Experts](https://developers.google.com/experts/all/technology/web-technologies)

*   [Official Website](https://www.ngxs.io/)
*   [GitHub Repo (‚≠ê3.6k)](https://github.com/ngxs/store) - NGXS tries to make things as simple and accessible as possible with less boilerplate and code to maintain.
*   [emitter (‚≠ê110)](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/emitter) - New pattern that provides the opportunity to feel free from actions.
*   [select-snapshot (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/select-snapshot) - Flexibile decorator that allows to get a snapshot of the state.
*   [actions-executing (‚≠ê27)](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/actions-executing) - This plugin allows you to easily know if an action is being executed and control UI elements or control flow of your code to execute.
*   [ngxs-synchronizers (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/lVlyke/ngxs-synchronizers) - Simplifies synchronizing your NGXS-based application state with external data sources.
*   [ngxs-message-plugin (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/Andreas-Hjortland/ngxs-message-plugin) - An NGXS plugin which allows you to share state between different browser contexts.
*   [firestore-plugin (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/firestore-plugin) - Firestore plugin for NGXS.
*   [ngxs-reset-plugin (‚≠ê108)](https://github.com/ng-turkey/ngxs-reset-plugin) - Reset plugin for NGXS: Effortlessly clears, resets, or overwrites NGXS states respecting the state tree.
*   [ngxs-state-mixins (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/zampage/ngxs-state-mixins) - Concept of how to implement state mixins in NGXS.

*   [ng2-tooltip-directive (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/cloudfactorydk/ng2-tooltip-directive) - Forked from [ng2-tooltip-directive (‚≠ê99)](https://github.com/drozhzhin-n-e/ng2-tooltip-directive).
*   [angular-tooltip (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/babybeet/angular-tooltip) - Easily show tooltips programmatically and/or declaratively in Angular.
*   [ngx-tippy-wrapper (‚≠ê62)](https://github.com/farengeyt451/ngx-tippy-wrapper) - Angular wrapper for [Tippy.js (‚≠ê12k)](https://github.com/atomiks/tippyjs).
*   [tooltip-testing (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/chandumaram/tooltip-testing) - Tooltip for Angular, forked from `cm-angular-tooltip`.
*   [angular-ellipsis-tooltip (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/wandri/angular-ellipsis-tooltip) - Angular component to display ellipsis and material tooltip dynamically.
